name:E‚Äçr‚Äçi‚Äçc‚ÄçM
info:Standard Single
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:18 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted December 19, 2021
msg:The room was a bit smaller than I was expecting. The pool looked great but I didn't use it. The bathtub was great and I easily fit in it. I'm iffy if I would stay again. 2 reasons. It's winter so I could not get the air-conditioning to actually cool off the room and I like cold rooms. So I had to open a window but neighboring construction started at 7am so that was unpleasant. Not the hotel's fault. With the windows closed I could barely hear anything, I just needed them open to keep the room cool. Second was that while the curtains in the room do a fair job of blocking sunlight, the curtain in the bathroom did not. There is a glass door between the bathroom and the bedroom, so the early morning sun had no problem making my room light. I like cold rooms and dark rooms so I can sleep in in the morning. I got neither of these. The location is great, and while I didn't eat at the restaurant due to other plans, the food smelled great. Wanting to try the pool and eat at the restaurants is definitely what would bring me back.  If I book again, I'll try to get a room with better curtains and hopefully a room that can be cooled (I know many hotels turn off the A/C in winter, so it's not just a problem here).
